about_this_resource_text: '<h2 class="subhead">Description</h2><p>In this lecture,
  Prof. Gruber uses the information taught in class to explain the real world example
  of health economics, and how it plays out in policy and practice. There is no handout
  for this lecture.&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Instructor: </strong>Prof. Jonathan Gruber</p><p>&nbsp;</p>'

  <span m="601810">the</span> <span m="601870">government,</span> <span m="602170">which</span>
  <span m="602290">I'll come</span> <span m="602500">to</span> <span m="602620">next,</span>
  <span m="603850">then</span> <span m="604090">you</span> <span m="604180">were</span>

  <span m="604990">fact</span> <span m="605290">that</span> <span m="605410">if</span>
  <span m="605500">you</span> <span m="605590">got</span> <span m="605830">sick,</span>

  <span m="608680">is</span> <span m="608740">sort</span> <span m="608890">of</span>
  <span m="608950">weird.</span> <span m="609220">Insurance</span> <span m="609520">is

  <span m="820540">these</span> <span m="820690">problems.</span> <span m="821890">And</span>
  <span m="822310">no</span> <span m="822580">one</span> <span m="822700">ever</span>
  <span m="822850">proposed</span> <span m="823120">subsidization</span> <span m="823630">big</span>
  <span m="823810">enough</span> <span m="823960">to</span> <span m="824050">overcome</span>
  <span m="824380">these</span> <span m="824530">problems.</span></p><p><span m="825270">In</span>
  <span m="825360">my</span> <span m="825500">MIT</span> <span m="825760">example,</span>
  <span m="826120">I</span> <span m="826150">was</span> <span m="826240">going</span>
  <span m="826360">to</span> <span m="826420">give</span> <span m="826510">$400</span>

  <span m="829060">people,</span> <span m="829330">which</span> <span m="829510">is</span>

  <span m="833050">It</span> <span m="833110">seems</span> <span m="833290">a</span>

  <span m="1410890">win,</span> <span m="1411090">everyone</span> <span m="1411310">would

  m="1412000">You'd</span> <span m="1412690">lose</span> <span m="1412930">money.</span></p><p><span
  m="1413200">So</span> <span m="1413650">you want</span> <span m="1413840">an</span>
  <span m="1413980">equal</span> <span m="1414250">distribution</span> <span m="1414730">of</span>
  <span m="1414850">risks.</span> <span m="1415730">So</span> <span m="1415810">what</span>
  <span m="1415930">you</span> <span m="1416050">want</span> <span m="1416230">is</span>
  <span m="1416320">you</span> <span m="1416410">want</span> <span m="1416530">to</span>
  <span m="1416590">set</span> <span m="1416740">the</span> <span m="1416830">point</span>
  <span m="1417100">spread</span> <span m="1417370">so the</span> <span m="1417460">distribution</span>
  <span m="1417910">of risk is</span> <span m="1418210">equal.</span> <span m="1418960">Then</span>
  <span m="1419110">having</span> <span m="1419350">done</span> <span m="1419530">that,</span>
  <span m="1419710">you</span> <span m="1419770">just</span> <span m="1419890">make</span>
  <span m="1420040">your</span> <span m="1420130">money</span> <span m="1420310">off</span>

  <span m="2176540">way</span> <span m="2176720">to</span> <span m="2176810">control--</span>
  <span m="2177680">the</span> <span m="2177770">third</span> <span m="2178040">regulatory</span>
  <span m="2178490">mechanism,</span> <span m="2179450">and</span> <span m="2179570">the</span>
  <span m="2179630">most</span> <span m="2179900">important,</span> <span m="2180830">is</span>
  <span m="2180980">price</span> <span m="2181340">regulation.</span> <span m="2183600">We</span>
  <span m="2183750">are</span> <span m="2183870">the</span> <span m="2183990">only</span>
  <span m="2184380">nation</span> <span m="2184720">in</span> <span m="2184800">the</span>
  <span m="2184890">world</span> <span m="2185880">which</span> <span m="2186090">essentially</span>
  <span m="2186570">lets</span> <span m="2186780">the</span> <span m="2186900">free</span>
  <span m="2187170">market</span> <span m="2187500">determine</span> <span m="2187890">the</span>
  <span m="2187950">price</span> <span m="2188280">of</span> <span m="2188370">health</span>
  <span m="2188550">care</span> <span m="2188670">services.</span> <span m="2190680">Every</span>
  <span m="2190980">other</span> <span m="2191190">nation</span> <span m="2191550">regulates</span>
  <span m="2192180">the</span> <span m="2192240">prices</span> <span m="2193260">that</span>
  <span m="2193380">people</span> <span m="2193650">pay</span> <span m="2193830">for</span>
  <span m="2193950">their</span> <span m="2194070">health</span> <span m="2194220">care</span>
  <span m="2194380">services.</span> <span m="2195970">Now</span> <span m="2196130">the</span>
  <span m="2196460">question</span> <span m="2196880">we</span> <span m="2196970">have</span>
  <span m="2197060">to</span> <span m="2197150">ask</span> <span m="2197480">is</span>
  <span m="2198140">why?</span> <span m="2199500">Why</span> <span m="2199680">does</span>
  <span m="2199800">that</span> <span m="2199920">make</span> <span m="2200100">sense?</span></p><p><span
  m="2200430">Well,</span> <span m="2200580">the</span> <span m="2200700">answer</span>
  <span m="2201090">would</span> <span m="2201240">be</span> <span m="2201960">that</span>
  <span m="2202140">we</span> <span m="2202260">think--</span> <span m="2203040">it</span>
  <span m="2203130">would</span> <span m="2203250">make</span> <span m="2203460">sense</span>
  <span m="2203760">if</span> <span m="2203940">we</span> <span m="2204060">think</span>

  <span m="2209480">And</span> <span m="2209630">in</span> <span m="2209720">fact,</span>
  <span m="2210780">it</span> <span m="2210880">turns</span> <span m="2211070">out</span>

  <span m="2212780">in</span> <span m="2212870">determination</span> <span m="2213320">of</span>
  <span m="2213380">health</span> <span m="2213550">care</span> <span m="2213680">prices.</span>
  <span m="2215110">So</span> <span m="2215290">one</span> <span m="2215680">market</span>
  <span m="2216010">failure,</span> <span m="2216280">for</span> <span m="2216400">example,</span>

  <span m="2219310">I</span> <span m="2219490">don't</span> <span m="2219730">know--</span>
  <span m="2220480">I</span> <span m="2220600">can't</span> <span m="2220870">shop</span>

  <span m="2227830">shop.</span></p><p><span m="2228940">It's</span> <span m="2229100">a</span>
  <span m="2229140">hard</span> <span m="2229480">market</span> <span m="2229630">to</span>
